WAVEFAZESLAMMER_PAGE1_TITLE=What is WaveFazeSlammer?

WAVEFAZESLAMMER_PAGE1_INFO=
The WaveFazeSlammer is an {#ffaa00}extremely advanced technique{#}
that combines {~}FOUR{/~} different movement abilities:

-{#00ff00}Wavedash{#} to gain horizontal momentum
-{#00ffff}Dream Dash{#} to phase through dream blocks
-{#ffff00}Wall Jump{#} to change direction mid-air
-{#ff00ff}Ground Pound Dash{#} to slam down with force

This technique requires {~}precise timing{/~} and
understanding of all the basic movement mechanics.
Master this, and {~}no obstacle{/~} can stop you!

WAVEFAZESLAMMER_PAGE2_TITLE=Step-by-Step Execution

WAVEFAZESLAMMER_PAGE2_STEPS=
{#00ff00}Step 1:{#} Perform a wavedash by dashing
diagonally down and jumping immediately

{#00ffff}Step 2:{#} While airborne, use dream dash
to phase through a dream block

{#ffff00}Step 3:{#} Wall jump off a nearby wall
to redirect your momentum

{#ff00ff}Step 4:{#} Dash diagonally down to perform
a ground pound slam for maximum impact

Perfect execution requires {~}rhythm and flow{/~}!

   {#666666}? You'll bonk into the wall{#}

{#ff0000}X{#} Forgetting to {~}wall jump{/~} after dream dash
   {#666666}? You won't have the angle for ground pound{#}

{#ff0000}X{#} Ground pounding {~}too early{/~}
   {#666666}? You'll miss your target{#}
